 sabase pehle ghar kii safai kar use svachh bana liya jaataa he

 iske pashchaat chhathvrati snaan kar satvik bhojan grahan kar vrath kii shuruyaat karte hai

 This is called 'kharna'

 isamen namak or chini kaa upyog nahin kiya jaataa he

 shashthee tithi ek vishesh khagauleey avasar he

 During monsoon there is a possibility of infection of many diseases
 inamen se kai bimariyon ke bare main tab tak pataa nahin chalata jab tak pareshaani bahut na bad jaae

 kuch ehtiyaat baratkar barsaat main hone vaali bimariyon or unase hone vaali pareshaaniyon se bachaa ja saktaa he
 Some common diseases and ways to avoid them: Influenza (cold and cold): The most common disease occurring in the monsoon
 kuch behad sankramak virus shwaas nalee ke upree hisse ko sankramit karte hai or is tarah naak or gale ko prabhavit karte hai
 Symptoms: stuffy nose, body ache, sore throat, cough and fever
 ilaajah doctor se poochkar hi koi dawa len
 Prevention: If there is a cold, the best thing to do is to take adequate amount of fluids, nutrients and a balanced diet
 isse sharir kaa immune system majboot hota he or rog se bachane main madad milti he
 For this, use fruits and green vegetables rich in vitamin C
 saath hi sankramit vyakti se dur rahen
 Dengue: This virus is spread due to tiger mosquito (aedes aegypti), which are born in the rainy season
 dengue ko ''haddi tod bukhaar" bhi kaha jaataa he
 Symptoms include joint and muscle pain, headache, fatigue and red marks on the body
 gambhir sthiti main pet main dard, sharir ke kisi bhi hisse se raktasrav or ''shock'" shaamil hai
 Treatment: There is no specific antibiotic or antiviral drug for this
 iske lakshanon kaa hi ilaaj hota he
 It is better to rest and take fluids
 dard or sujan ke liye kisi bhi tarah kii dawa lene se pehle doctor kii salaah avashya len kyonki inase raktasrav kaa andeshaa rahata he
 Sometimes hospitalization may be advised
 bachaavaru machharon ko apane irdagird na panpane den

 Prevention: In the area affected by malaria, take anti-malarial drugs beforehand as a precaution
 machharon ko dur rakhane vaali kriim lagaaein

 lakshanh antra shoth main aam taur par pet main anthan, michali, ulti or dast kii shikaayat hoti he

 Prevention: Do not eat raw foods such as salads etc
 because sometimes they are not cleaned properly and are not kept at the right temperature
 sadak ke kinare ke khan-paan se bachein

 viral hepatitisoliver kii yah beemaari dooshit aahaar or pani ke kaaran failati he

 unhen laga ki 4,000 ru

 mil gaye

" '' modi lahar par savaar nae yug main pravesh kar chuki bijepi kaa nayaa santhnik prayog kaaryakartaaon ke liye achraj kii baat he to shaayad bijepi ke rashtriya adhyaksh amit shah kii vah tis bhi jahaan desh kii rajdhani main arvind kejariwal jaise raajnneeti ke nausikhue ne bijepi ko teen siton tak samet diya
 Actually, BJP has changed the nature of Delhi BJP by appointing Tiwari
 dilli bijepi main amuman punjabi-baniyon kaa varchasv mana jaataa rahaa he
 But this time, betting on the changed population equations has been played in Delhi by assigning leadership to a face from the east
 ek varisht netaa bataate hai ki dilli kii kul 70 vidhansabha or saat loksabhaa siton main aabaadi kii sanrachana main badlaav aa chukaa he
 According to BJP leaders, if the Ring Road is to be considered a measure, before the 2003 delimitation, out of 70 assembly seats in Delhi, 50 seats were inside and 20 were outside
 isi tarah loksabhaa kii 5 siten andar thim to do baahar
 But after the delimitation, the situation changed rapidly and within the Ring Road, 20 Assembly and two Lok Sabha seats were left
 bijepi netaaon kaa maananaa he ki kejariwal ne is badale hue sameekaran kaa achche se adhyayan kiya tha or autowalon ke saath-saath slam aria par focus kiya

 ab bijepi kii ranneeti manoj tiwari ke chehre ko saamne rakhkar purvanchal vot ko waapas laane kii he

 manoj tiwari ke vyaktitv kaa apana aakarshan he or ve hamaare star prachaarkon main rahe hai

" bijepi main vyakti vishesh se nahin balki team se sanghathan chalata he

 lekin in sawaalon ke baavjood 45 varshiya tiwari rajnatik jhanjhawaton se jujhane ko taiyaar hai

 multah bihar ke camoor jile ke ataravaliya ke rahane vaale tiwari kaa janm varanasi ke sarkari aspataal main hua tha

 Says Tiwari, a graduate in history from BHU, "I have taken admission in every course of life by giving competition and i am doing the same today
" '' tiwari ko ehsaas he ki un par gaiyr aresas vaala hone kaa thappa laga he, lekin ve bataate hai ki 1991 main ve akhil bhartiya vidhyaarthee parishad ke saadhaaran sadsy bane the or chaatrasangh chunaav main parishad ke ummidavaar ke prastaavak bane the jo vahaan record main darj he
 Unaware of the questions arising due to being from the film world, Tiwari says, "my philosophy only reflects in my film
 maine bhrashtachar, berogari, bhrun hatya, kargil yuddh jaise muddon par geet likhe or gaae hai to filmein bhi jivan kii sachhee ghatnaon par kii hai

 2009 main unhone samaajawaadee party ke tikat par gorakhpur se loksabhaa chunaav ladaa tha

 lekin bijepi main aane kii vajah or prerana ve sirf narendra modi ko maanate hai

 usase pehle unhone modi ko kabhi saamne se nahin dekha tha
 On that stage, Modi said to Tiwari, "manoj bhai, how are you?" Tiwari says, "I can't forget that moment
 modi ji ne mujhe pehle kabhi nahin dekha tha, phir bhi naam lekar pukaara

 usee din tay kar liya ki mujhe is vyakti (modi) ke saath chalanaa he
 "not only this, Tiwari credits Modi for the new innings of politics in this way," i see the thought of Yugapurusha in every action of Modi and i never feel that i am in a political party
 balki mujhe lagata he ki main raja rammohan raay jaise samaaj sudhaarak kii team main hum
 Citing that there is no time to do the film, Tiwari wants to make the song an weapon to take society in the right direction instead of business
 haalanki unka maananaa he ki 20 reliyon se jo sandesh diya ja saktaa he, use ek film ke jariye kaha ja saktaa he

 unke agle din kaa program raat main sone se pehle taiyaar ho jaataa he or usee hisaab se unki dincharya tay hoti he
